NOTICE ...

NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

V. PADMAPRIYA,

AUTOMOTIVE INFOTRONICS LIMITED
Registered Office: No. 1 Sardar Patel Road, Guindy, Chennai-600 032,
(Publication in pursuance of Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956)

Notice is hereby given in general information that the members of Automotive Infotronics Limited, at an Extraordinary
General Meeting of the Company held on Thursday the 6th day of March, 2014 at its Registered Office have passed the
following special resolution to wind up the above Company Voluntarily
“RESOLVED that pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1) (b) and all other applicable provisions of the Companies
Act, 1956, the consent of the members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company
as the Members’ Voluntary Winding Up.”
(BY Order of the Board)
Chennai,
14th March 2014.

B. JANANEE
Company Secretary.
